            "recommendationService.js": "const { QUESTION_BANK, toLeetCodeUrl } = require(\"../data/dsaQuestionBank\");\n\r\nfunction shuffle(array) {\r\n  const copy = array.slice();\r\n  for (let i = copy.length - 1; i > 0; i -= 1) {\r\n    const j = Math.floor(Math.random() * (i + 1));\r\n    [copy[i], copy[j]] = [copy[j], copy[i]];\r\n  }\r\n  return copy;\r\n}\r\n\r\nfunction normaliseTopic(s) {\r\n  return String(s || \"\")\r\n    .trim()\r\n    .toLowerCase();\r\n}\r\n\r\n// Maps the frontend's heuristic topics to the curated bank topics.\r\nconst TOPIC_MAP = {\r\n  graph: [\"Graphs\", \"BFS\", \"DFS\"],\r\n  trie: [\"Design Data Structure\"],\r\n  backtracking: [\"Backtracking\"],\r\n  \"dynamic programming\": [\"Dynamic Programming\"],\r\n  tree: [\"Trees\"],\r\n  \"depth-first search\": [\"DFS\"],\r\n  \"binary search\": [\"Modified Binary Search\"],\r\n  array: [\"Two Pointers\", \"Sliding Window\", \"Prefix Sum\"],\r\n  string: [\"Sliding Window\", \"Two Pointers\"],\r\n  \"hash table\": [\"Sliding Window\", \"Prefix Sum\"],\r\n};\r\n\r\nfunction pickTopicsFromWeakAreas(weakAreas) {\r\n  const desired = [];\r\n  for (const area of weakAreas || []) {\r\n    const mapped = TOPIC_MAP[normaliseTopic(area)];\r\n    if (mapped?.length) desired.push(...mapped);\r\n  }\r\n  return Array.from(new Set(desired));\r\n}\r\n\r\nfunction indexBank() {\n  const byTopic = new Map();\n  for (const bucket of QUESTION_BANK) {\n    byTopic.set(bucket.topic, bucket);\n  }\n  return byTopic;\r\n}\r\n\r\n/**\r\n * Returns grouped limit = 20 } = {}) {\r\n  const byTopic = indexBank();\r\n\r\n  const topics = pickTopicsFromWeakAreas(weakAreas);\r\n  const topicsToUse = topics.length ? topics : Array.from(byTopic.keys());\r\n\r\n  const chosen = new Set();\r\n  const grouped = {};\r\n\r\n  // Pre-shuffle each topic's list so we don't always return the same order.\r\n  const topicQueues = topicsToUse\r\n    .map((t) => byTopic.get(t))\r\n    .filter(Boolean)\r\n    .map((bucket) => ({\r\n      topic: bucket.topic,\r\n      description: bucket.description,\r\n      queue: shuffle(bucket.problems),\r\n    }));\r\n\r\n  // Round-robin across topics until we hit limit.\r\n  let safety = 0;\r\n  while (chosen.size < limit && topicQueues.length && safety < 10_000) {\r\n    safety += 1;\r\n    let progressed = false;\r\n\r\n    for (const tq of topicQueues) {\r\n      if (chosen.size >= limit) break;\r\n      const next = tq.queue.pop();\r\n      if (!next) continue;\r\n\r\n      const key = `${tq.topic}::${next.name}`.toLowerCase();\r\n      if (chosen.has(key)) continue;\r\n\r\n      progressed = true;\r\n      chosen.add(key);\r\n\r\n      const problem = {\r\n        name: next.name,\r\n        problemName: next.name,\r\n        difficulty: next.difficulty || \"Medium\",\r\n        leetcodeUrl: toLeetCodeUrl(next),\r\n        comment: tq.description,\r\n      };\r\n\r\n      if (!grouped[tq.topic]) grouped[tq.topic] = [];\r\n      grouped[tq.topic].push(problem);\r\n    }\r\n\r\n    if (!progressed) break;\r\n  }\r\n\r\n  // Ensure at most `limit` total if a topic got extra (shouldn't happen, but safe).\r\n  let count = 0;\r\n  for (const topic of Object.keys(grouped)) {\r\n    const remaining = limit - count;\r\n    if (remaining <= 0) {\r\n      delete grouped[topic];\r\n      continue;\r\n    }\r\n    if (grouped[topic].length > remaining)\r\n      grouped[topic] = grouped[topic].slice(0, remaining);\r\n    count += grouped[topic].length;\r\n  }\r\n\r\n  return grouped;\n}\n\nfunction getQuestionBankForTopic(topic) {\n  if (!topic) return null;\n  const byTopic = indexBank();\n  const bucket = byTopic.get(String(topic).trim());\n  if (!bucket) return null;\n\n  return {\n    topic: bucket.topic,\n    description: bucket.description,\n    problems: bucket.problems.map((problem) => ({\n      name: problem.name,\n      problemName: problem.name,\n      difficulty: problem.difficulty || \"Medium\",\n      leetcodeUrl: toLeetCodeUrl(problem),\n      comment: bucket.description,\n    })),\n  };\n}\n\nmodule.exports = {\n  getQuestionBankForTopic,\n  getTopicWiseRecommendations,\n};\n"

            "database.js": "const { Sequelize } = require(\"sequelize\");\nconst dns = require(\"dns\");\nconst { Resolver } = require(\"dns\");\n\nconst resolver = new Resolver();\nresolver.setServers([\"8.8.8.8\", \"8.8.4.4\"]);\ndns.setDefaultResultOrder(\"ipv4first\");\nconst defaultLookup = dns.lookup.bind(dns);\n\ndns.lookup = (hostname, options, callback) => {\n  if (typeof options === \"function\") {\n    callback = options;\n    options = {};\n  }\n\n  resolver.resolve4(hostname, (err, addresses) => {\n    if (!err && addresses && addresses.length > 0) {\n      callback(null, addresses[0], 4);\n      return;\n    }\n\n    defaultLookup(hostname, options, callback);\n  });\n};\n\nconst originalSocketConnect = require(\"net\").Socket.prototype.connect;\nrequire(\"net\").Socket.prototype.connect = function (\n  portOrOpts,\n  hostOrCb,\n  ...rest\n) {\n  if (typeof portOrOpts === \"number\") {\n    const host = typeof hostOrCb === \"string\" ? hostOrCb : \"localhost\";\n    const cb = typeof hostOrCb === \"function\" ? hostOrCb : rest[0];\n    return originalSocketConnect.apply(\n      this,\n      cb\n        ?             "leetcodeListService.js": "const axios = require(\"axios\");\nconst cheerio = require(\"cheerio\");\nconst pLimit = require(\"p-limit\");\nconst LeetCodeProblemCache = }\n\n  const match = parsedUrl.pathname.match(\n    /^(?:\\/u\\/[^/]+)?\\/problem-list\\/([^/]+)\\/?$/i,\n  );\n  if (!match?.[1]) {\n    throw new Error(\"Invalid URL\");\n  }\n\n  return /\"titleSlug\"\\s*:\\s*\"([a-z0-9]+(?:-[a-z0-9]+)*)\"/gi;\n  const questionSlugPattern =\n    /\"questionTitleSlug\"\\s*:\\s*\"([a-z0-9]+(?:-[a-z0-9]+)*)\"/gi;\n\n  for (const pattern of [pathPattern, titleSlugPattern, questionSlugPattern]) {\n    for (const match of markup.matchAll(pattern)) {\n      if (match?.[1]) {\n        discovered.push(match[1]);\n      }\n    }\n  }\n\n  return normalizeTitleSlugs(discovered);\n}\n\nasync function fetchListViaApi(listSlug) {\n  const favoriteQuestionList = await getFavoriteQuestionList(listSlug);\n  const questions = ...DEFAULT_HEADERS,\n        Accept: \"text/html,application/xhtml+xml,application/xml;q=0.9,image/avif,image/webp,*/*;q=0.8\",\n      },\n      timeout: 15000,\n    });\n  } catch (error) {\n    if Add LEETCODE_COOKIE/LEETCODE_CSRFTOKEN in the backend env or use a machine/network that can reach LeetCode.\",\n      );\n    }\n    throw error;\n  }\n  const $ = cheerio.load(response.data || \"\");\n  const collectedSlugs = extractProblemSlugsFromHtml(response.data);\n\n  $(\"a[href]\").each((_, element) => {\n    const href = $(element).attr(\"href\");\n    const match = String(href || \"\").match(/^\\/problems\\/([a-z0-9-]+)\\/?$/i);\n    if (match?.[1]) {\n      collectedSlugs.push(match[1]);\n    }\n  });\n\n  const titleSlugs = normalizeTitleSlugs(collectedSlugs);\n\n  if (titleSlugs.length === 0) {\n    throw new Error(\n      \"Private list or scraping fallback could not find any problem slugs\",\n    );\n  }\n\n  console.info(`[leetcode-list] Source=scraping slug=${listSlug} count=${titleSlugs.length}`);\n\n  return {\n    source: \"scraping\",\n    title: listSlug,\n    questions: titleSlugs.map((titleSlug) => ({\n      title: \"\",\n      titleSlug,\n      difficulty: \"\",\n    })),\n  };\n}\n\nasync function resolveListQuestions({ listUrl, listSlug }) {\n  try {\n    return await fetchListViaApi(listSlug);\n  } catch (error) {\n    console.warn(\n      `[leetcode-list] API failed for slug=${listSlug}. );\n}\n\nfunction formatProblemOutput(problem) {\n  const exampleLines = String(problem.exampleTestcases || \"\")\n    .split(\"\\n\")\n    .map((line) => line.trim())\n    .filter(Boolean);\n\n             "revisionListParser.js": "const DIFFICULTY_MAP = new Map([\n  [\"easy\", \"Easy\"],\n  [\"easy.\", \"Easy\"],\n  [\"med\", \"Medium\"],\n  [\"med.\", \"Medium\"],\n  [\"medium\", (accumulator, problem) => {\n      if (problem.difficulty === \"Easy\") accumulator.easy += 1;\n      if (problem.difficulty === \"Medium\") accumulator.medium += 1;\n      if (problem.difficulty === JSON.parse(options.body) : undefined,\r\n      timeout: 30000,\r\n      validateStatus: () => true,\r\n    });\r\n\r\n    if (response.status < 200 || response.status >= 300) {\r\n      const data = response.data;\r\n      const message =\r\n        (data && typeof data === \"object\" && (data.error || data.message)) ||\r\n        response.statusText ||\r\n        \"Request failed\";\r\n      throw new Error(message);\r\n    }\r\n\r\n    return response.data;\r\n  } catch (error) {\r\n    const message =\r\n      error?.response?.data?.error ||\r\n      error?.response?.data?.message ||\r\n      error?.message ||\r\n      \"Request failed\";\r\n    throw new Error(message);\r\n  }\r\n}\r\n\r\nasync function requestJsonWithFallback(urls, options = {}) {\n  let lastError = null;\n\r\n  for (const url of urls) {\r\n    try {\r\n      return await requestJson(url, options);\r\n    } catch (error) {\r\n      lastError = error;\r\n    }\r\n  }\r\n\r\n  throw new Error(lastError?.message || \"Request failed\");\n}\n\nasync function mapWithConcurrency(items, worker, concurrency = 4) {\n  const queue = [...items];\n  const results = [];\n\n  async function runWorker() {\n    while (queue.length > 0) {\n      const item = queue.shift();\n      results.push(await worker(item));\n    }\n  }\n\n  const workerCount = Math.min(concurrency, items.length);\n  await Promise.all(\n    Array.from({ length: workerCount }, () => runWorker()),\n  );\n\n  return results;\n}\n\r\nfunction toSlug(text) {\r\n  return (text || \"\")\r\n    .toLowerCase()\r\n    .replace(/[^a-z0-9]+/g, \"-\")\r\n    .replace(/^-+|-+$/g, \"\")\r\n    .replace(/-{2,}/g, \"-\");\r\n}\r\n\r\nfunction extractSlugCandidatesFromTitle(videoTitle) {\r\n  const candidates = [];\r\n  const unique = new Set();\r\n\r\n  const fromUrl = [\r\n    ...videoTitle.matchAll(/leetcode\\.com\\/problems\\/([a-z0-9-]+)/gi),\r\n  ]\r\n    .map((m) => m[1]?.toLowerCase())\r\n    .filter(Boolean);\r\n\r\n  const pieces = videoTitle\r\n    .split(/[|:]/)\r\n    .map((p) => p.trim())\r\n    .filter(Boolean)\r\n    .slice(0, 4);\r\n\r\n  for (const raw of [...fromUrl, ...pieces]) {\r\n    const cleaned = raw\r\n      .replace(/\\([^)]*\\)/g, \" \")\r\n      .replace(/\\[[^\\]]*\\]/g, \" \")\r\n      .replace(\r\n        /\\b(leetcode|problem|solution|tutorial|explained|dsa|hindi|english|shorts?)\\b/gi,\r\n        \" \",\r\n      )\r\n      .replace(/\\s+/g, \" \")\r\n      .trim();\r\n\r\n    if (!cleaned) continue;\r\n\r\n    const slug = toSlug(cleaned.replace(/^\\d+[\\.)\\-:\\s]+/, \"\"));\r\n    if (!slug || slug.length < 3 || unique.has(slug)) continue;\r\n\r\n    unique.add(slug);\r\n    candidates.push(slug);\r\n  }\r\n\r\n  return candidates;\r\n}\r\n\r\nfunction extractLeetCodeFrontendId(videoTitle) {\r\n  const patterns = [\r\n    /(?:leetcode|lc)\\s*#?\\s*(\\d{1,4})\\b/i,\r\n    /\\b(?:problem|ques(?:tion)?)\\s*#?\\s*(\\d{1,4})\\b/i,\r\n    /\\b#(\\d{1,4})\\b/,\r\n    /\\b(\\d{1,4})\\s*[.\\-:|]\\s*[a-z]/i,\r\n  ];\r\n\r\n  for (const pattern of patterns) {\r\n    const match = videoTitle.match(pattern);\r\n    if (!match?.[1]) continue;\r\n\r\n    const id = String(match[1]).trim();\r\n    const numeric = Number(id);\r\n    if (!numeric || numeric < 1 || numeric > 4000) continue;\r\n    return String(numeric);\r\n  }\r\n\r\n  return null;\r\n}\r\n\r\n/**\r\n * POST /api/youtube-playlist/import\r\n * Body: { playlistUrl: string }\r\n *\r\n * Full pipeline:\r\n *  1. Fetch video list from YouTube API\r\n *  2. For each video title → ask OpenAI to identify LeetCode problem\r\n *  3. Fetch full problem data from LeetCode GraphQL\r\n *  4. Store sheet + problems in PostgreSQL\r\n *  5. Return { sheetId }\r\n */\r\nasync function importPlaylist(req, res) {\r\n  const { playlistUrl } = req.body;\r\n  const userId = req.headers[\"x-user-id\"];\r\n\r\n  if (!userId) {\r\n    return res.status(401).json({ error: \"Unauthorized\" });\r\n  }\r\n\r\n  if (!playlistUrl || !playlistUrl.trim()) {\r\n    return res.status(400).json({ error: \"playlistUrl is required\" });\r\n  }\r\n\r\n  try {\r\n    // ── Step 1: Fetch playlist videos from YouTube ──────────────────────\r\n    console.log(`[Playlist Import] Fetching videos from: ${playlistUrl}`);\r\n    const videos = await fetchPlaylistVideos(playlistUrl);\r\n\r\n    if (!videos || videos.length === 0) {\r\n      return res\r\n        .status(404)\r\n        .json({ error: \"No videos found in this playlist\" });\r\n    }\r\n    console.log(`[Playlist Import] Found ${videos.length} videos`);\r\n\r\n    // ── Step 2: Create the Learning Sheet record ─────────────────────────\r\n    const sheetName = `DSA Sheet — ${new Date().toLocaleDateString(\"en-US\", {\r\n      month: \"short\",\r\n      day: \"numeric\",\r\n      year: \"numeric\",\r\n    })}`;\r\n\r\n    const sheet = await LearningSheet.create({\r\n      userId,\r\n      name: sheetName,\r\n      playlist_url: playlistUrl,\r\n    });\r\n\r\n    // ── Step 3: Process each video through OpenAI + LeetCode ─────────────\r\n    const results = [];\r\n    const savedSlugs = new Set();\r\n\r\n    for (const video of videos) {\r\n      try {\r\n        console.log(`[Playlist Import] Processing: \"${video.videoTitle}\"`);\r\n\r\n        let identified = null;\r\n        let problemData = null;\r\n        let matchConfidence = 0;\r\n\r\n        // Step 3.1 - Build deterministic candidate list from title keywords.\r\n        const titleCandidates = await findProblemCandidatesByTitle(\r\n          video.videoTitle,\r\n          8,\r\n        );\r\n        const topCandidate = titleCandidates[0] || null;\r\n\r\n        // Step 3.2 - Strong deterministic signal: explicit LeetCode problem id.\r\n        if (!problemData) {\r\n          const frontendId =\r\n            extractLeetCodeFrontendId(video.videoTitle) ||\r\n            (topCandidate?.score >= 0.9 ? topCandidate.frontendId : null);\r\n\r\n          if (frontendId) {\r\n            const byId = await fetchProblemByFrontendId(frontendId);\r\n            if (byId) {\r\n              problemData = byId;\r\n              matchConfidence = Math.max(matchConfidence, 0.9);\r\n              identified = {\r\n                title: byId.title,\r\n                titleSlug: byId.titleSlug,\r\n                difficulty: byId.difficulty,\r\n                confidence: matchConfidence,\r\n              };\r\n              console.log(\r\n                `[Playlist Import] ID/candidate fallback matched \"${video.videoTitle}\" -> ${byId.titleSlug}`,\r\n              );\r\n            }\r\n          }\r\n        }\r\n\r\n        // Step 3.3 - High-quality deterministic title match.\r\n        if (!problemData && topCandidate?.score >= 0.96) {\r\n          const byTopTitle = await fetchProblemBySlug(topCandidate.titleSlug);\r\n          if (byTopTitle) {\r\n            problemData = byTopTitle;\r\n            matchConfidence = Math.max(matchConfidence, topCandidate.score);\r\n            identified = {\r\n              title: byTopTitle.title,\r\n              titleSlug: byTopTitle.titleSlug,\r\n              difficulty: byTopTitle.difficulty,\r\n              confidence: matchConfidence,\r\n            };\r\n            console.log(\r\n              `[Playlist Import] Title candidate matched \"${video.videoTitle}\" -> ${byTopTitle.titleSlug} (${topCandidate.score})`,\r\n            );\r\n          }\r\n        }\r\n\r\n        // Step 3.4 - Ask DeepSeek with candidate context to reduce hallucinations.\r\n        if (!problemData) {\r\n          identified = await identifyLeetCodeProblem(video.videoTitle, {\r\n            candidateProblems: titleCandidates,\r\n          });\r\n          matchConfidence = Math.max(\r\n            matchConfidence,\r\n            identified?.confidence ?? 0,\r\n          );\r\n\r\n          if (identified?.titleSlug) {\r\n            problemData = await fetchProblemBySlug(identified.titleSlug);\r\n          }\r\n\r\n          if (!problemData && identified?.frontendId) {\r\n            const byAiId = await fetchProblemByFrontendId(\r\n              identified.frontendId,\r\n            );\r\n            if (byAiId) {\r\n              problemData = byAiId;\r\n              matchConfidence = Math.max(matchConfidence, 0.82);\r\n            }\r\n          }\r\n        }\r\n\r\n        // Fallback: derive likely slug candidates from title text\r\n        if (!problemData) {\r\n          const slugCandidates = extractSlugCandidatesFromTitle(\r\n            video.videoTitle,\r\n          );\r\n          for (const slug of slugCandidates) {\r\n            if (slug === identified?.titleSlug) continue;\r\n            const candidateProblem = await fetchProblemBySlug(slug);\r\n            if (candidateProblem) {\r\n              problemData = candidateProblem;\r\n              matchConfidence = Math.max(matchConfidence, 0.55);\r\n              if (!identified || !identified.titleSlug) {\r\n                identified = {\r\n                  title: candidateProblem.title,\r\n                  titleSlug: candidateProblem.titleSlug,\r\n                  difficulty: candidateProblem.difficulty,\r\n                  confidence: matchConfidence,\r\n                };\r\n              }\r\n              console.log(\r\n                `[Playlist Import] Fallback matched \"${video.videoTitle}\" -> ${candidateProblem.titleSlug}`,\r\n              );\r\n              break;\r\n            }\r\n          }\r\n        }\r\n\r\n        // Fallback: choose best fuzzy candidate if score is reasonably strong.\r\n        if (!problemData && topCandidate?.score >= 0.62) {\r\n          const byBestCandidate = await fetchProblemBySlug(\r\n            topCandidate.titleSlug,\r\n          );\r\n          if (byBestCandidate) {\r\n            problemData = byBestCandidate;\r\n            matchConfidence = Math.max(matchConfidence, topCandidate.score);\r\n            if (!identified || !identified.titleSlug) {\r\n              identified = {\r\n                title: byBestCandidate.title,\r\n                titleSlug: byBestCandidate.titleSlug,\r\n                difficulty: byBestCandidate.difficulty,\r\n                confidence: matchConfidence,\r\n              };\r\n            }\r\n            console.log(\r\n              `[Playlist Import] Fuzzy fallback matched \"${video.videoTitle}\" -> ${byBestCandidate.titleSlug} (${topCandidate.score})`,\r\n            );\r\n          }\r\n        }\r\n\r\n        // Skip if we still don't have a match and AI confidence is low.\r\n        if (\r\n          !problemData &&\r\n          (!identified || !identified.titleSlug || matchConfidence < 0.5)\r\n        ) {\r\n          console.log(\r\n            `[Playlist Import] Skipping \"${video.videoTitle}\" — no match or low confidence (${matchConfidence})`,\r\n          );\r\n          continue;\r\n        }\r\n\r\n        if (problemData && savedSlugs.has(problemData.titleSlug)) {\r\n          console.log(\r\n            `[Playlist Import] Duplicate slug skipped for \"${video.videoTitle}\" -> ${problemData.titleSlug}`,\r\n          );\r\n          continue;\r\n        }\r\n\r\n        if (!problemData) {\r\n          // Only save minimal entry if AI was highly confident (≥0.8)\r\n          // so we don't pollute the sheet with questionable matches\r\n          if (matchConfidence >= 0.8) {\r\n            const saved = await SheetProblem.create({\r\n              userId,\r\n              sheet_id: sheet.id,\r\n              title: identified.title,\r\n              title_slug: identified.titleSlug,\r\n              leetcode_link: `https://leetcode.com/problems/${identified.titleSlug}/`,\r\n              youtube_link: video.videoUrl,\r\n              difficulty: identified.difficulty,\r\n              description: \"\",\r\n              starter_code: \"\",\r\n              confidence_score: matchConfidence,\r\n            });\r\n            results.push(saved);\r\n            savedSlugs.add(identified.titleSlug);\r\n          } else {\r\n            console.log(\r\n              `[Playlist Import] Skipping \"${video.videoTitle}\" — LeetCode fetch failed and confidence too low`,\r\n            );\r\n          }\r\n          continue;\r\n        }\r\n\r\n        // Step 3.3 — Persist to database\r\n        const saved = await SheetProblem.create({\r\n          userId,\r\n          sheet_id: sheet.id,\r\n          title: problemData.title,\r\n          title_slug: problemData.titleSlug,\r\n          leetcode_link: problemData.leetcodeLink,\r\n          youtube_link: video.videoUrl,\r\n          difficulty: problemData.difficulty,\r\n          description: problemData.description,\r\n          starter_code: problemData.starterCode,\r\n          confidence_score: matchConfidence,\r\n        });\r\n\r\n        results.push(saved);\r\n        savedSlugs.add(problemData.titleSlug);\r\n      } catch (innerErr) {\r\n        console.error(\r\n          `[Playlist Import] Error on video \"${video.videoTitle}\":`,\r\n          innerErr.message,\r\n        );\r\n        // Swallow per-video errors so one failure doesn't abort the whole import\r\n      }\r\n    }\r\n\r\n    console.log(\r\n      `[Playlist Import] Done. Saved ${results.length} problems for sheet ${sheet.id}`,\r\n    );\r\n\r\n    // ── Step 4: Return the sheet ID ───────────────────────────────────────\r\n    return res.status(201).json({\r\n      sheetId: sheet.id,\r\n      sheetName: sheet.name,\r\n      totalVideos: videos.length,\r\n      savedProblems: results.length,\r\n    });\r\n  } catch (err) {\r\n    console.error(\"[Playlist Import] Fatal error:\", err.message);\r\n    return res\r\n      .status(500)\r\n      .json({ error: err.message || \"Internal server error\" });\r\n  }\r\n}\r\n\r\n/**\r\n * GET /api/youtube-playlist/sheet/:id\r\n * Returns a single sheet with all its problems.\r\n */\r\nasync function getSheet(req, res) {\r\n  const { id } = req.params;\r\n  const userId = req.headers[\"x-user-id\"];\r\n\r\n  if (!userId) {\r\n    return res.status(401).json({ error: \"Unauthorized\" });\r\n  }\r\n\r\n  try {\r\n    const sheet = await LearningSheet.findOne({ where: { id, userId } });\r\n    if (!sheet) {\r\n      return res.status(404).json({ error: \"Sheet not found\" });\r\n    }\r\n\r\n    const problems = await SheetProblem.findAll({\r\n      where: { err.message);\r\n    return res.status(500).json({ error: \"Failed to fetch sheet\" });\r\n  }\r\n}\r\n\r\n/**\r\n * GET /api/youtube-playlist/sheets\r\n * Returns all sheets (for listing).\r\n */\r\nasync function getAllSheets(req, res) {\r\n  const userId = req.headers[\"x-user-id\"];\r\n\r\n  if (!userId) {\r\n    return res.status(401).json({ error: \"Unauthorized\" });\r\n  }\r\n\r\n  try {\r\n    const sheets = await LearningSheet.findAll({\r\n      where: { userId },\r\n      order: [[\"id\", \"DESC\"]],\r\n    });\r\n    return res.json({ sheets });\r\n  } catch (err) {\r\n    console.error(\"[Get All Sheets] Error:\", err.message);\r\n    return res.status(500).json({ error: \"Failed to fetch sheets\" });\r\n  }\r\n}\r\n\r\nasync function renameSheet(req, res) {\r\n  const { id } = req.params;\r\n  const { name } = req.body || {};\r\n  const userId = req.headers[\"x-user-id\"];\r\n  const trimmedName = String(name || \"\").trim();\r\n\r\n  if (!userId) {\r\n    return trimmedName;\r\n    await sheet.save();\r\n\r\n    return res.json({ sheet });\r\n  } catch (err) {\r\n    console.error(\"[Rename Sheet] Error:\", err.message);\r\n    return res.status(500).json({ {\r\n  const { id } = req.params;\r\n  const userId = req.headers[\"x-user-id\"];\r\n\r\n  if (!userId) {\r\n    return res.status(401).json({ error: \"Unauthorized\" });\r\n  }\r\n\r\n  try {\r\n    await SheetProblem.destroy({ where: { sheet_id: id, userId } });\r\n    await LearningSheet.destroy({ where: { id, userId } });\r\n    return res.json({ message: \"Sheet deleted successfully\" });\r\n /api/youtube-playlist/sheet/:id/create-folder\r\n * Creates a folder in the file explorer for this sheet,\r\n * and a file for each problem. Each file is pre-populated\r\n * with the problem data (description, starter code, difficulty, etc.)\r\n * so it opens ready-to-use in the ProblemWorkspace editor.\r\n */\r\nasync function createFolderFromSheet(req, res) {\r\n  const { id } = req.params;\r\n  const userId = req.headers[\"x-user-id\"];\r\n\r\n  if (!userId) {\r\n    return res.status(401).json({ error: \"Unauthorized\" });\r\n  }\r\n\r\n  try {\r\n    // 1 ── Fetch the sheet + its problems ─────────────────────────────────\r\n    const sheet = await LearningSheet.findOne({ where: { id, userId } });\r\n    if (!sheet) {\r\n      return res.status(404).json({ error: \"Sheet not found\" });\r\n    }\r\n\r\n    const problems = await SheetProblem.findAll({\r\n      where: { sheet_id: id, userId },\r\n      order: [[\"id\", \"ASC\"]],\r\n    });\r\n\r\n    if (!problems.length) {\r\n      return res\r\n        .status(400)\r\n        .json({ error: \"Sheet has no problems to create files for\" });\r\n    }\r\n\r\n    // 2 ── Create folder in file-service ──────────────────────────────────\r\n    const folderRes = await requestJsonWithFallback(FILE_SERVICE_URLS, {\r\n      method: \"POST\",\r\n      body: JSON.stringify({\r\n        name: sheet.name,\r\n        type: \"folder\",\r\n        parentId: null,\r\n      }),\r\n      headers: { \"x-user-id\": userId },\r\n    });\r\n    const folderId = folderRes.id;\r\n    console.log(\r\n      `[Create Folder] Created folder \"${sheet.name}\" with id ${folderId}`,\r\n    );\r\n\r\n    // 3 ── Create a file for each problem name: problem.title,\n              type: \"file\",\n              parentId: folderId,\n              link: problem.leetcode_link || \"\",\n            }),\n            headers: { \"x-user-id\": userId },\n          });\n          const fileId = fileRes.id;\n\n          // Build codeSnippets array from the stored starter_code\n          const codeSnippets = problem.starter_code\n            ? [\n                {\n                  lang: \"JavaScript\",\n                  langSlug: \"javascript\",\n                  code: problem.starter_code,\n                },\n                {\n                  lang: \"Python3\",\n                  langSlug: \"python3\",\n                  code: problem.starter_code,\n                },\n              ]\n            : [];\n\n          // Update the problem entry with all stored data\n          const problemUrls = PROBLEM_SERVICE_URLS.map(\n            (baseUrl) => `${baseUrl}/${fileId}`,\n          );\n\n          await requestJsonWithFallback(problemUrls, {\n            method: \"PUT\",\n            body: JSON.stringify({\n              title: problem.title,\n              slug: problem.title_slug,\n              difficulty: problem.difficulty,\n              description: problem.description || \"\",\n              exampleTestcases: \"\",\n              tags: [],\n              codeSnippets,\n            }),\n            headers: { \"x-user-id\": userId },\n          });\n\n          console.log(\n            `[Create Folder] Created file \"${problem.title}\" (fileId ${fileId})`,\n          );\n\n          return { ok: true, fileId, title: problem.title };\n        } catch (innerErr) {\n          console.error(\n            `[Create Folder] Failed for problem \"${problem.title}\":`,\n            innerErr.message,\n          );\n\n          return {\n            ok: false,\n            title: problem.title,\n            error: innerErr.message,\n          };\n        }\n      },\n      4,\n    );\n\n    const createdFiles = fileResults\n      .filter((result) => result.ok)\n      .map(({ fileId, title }) => ({ fileId, title }));\n    const filesCreated = createdFiles.length;\n\n    return res.status(201).json({\n      folderId,\n      folderName: sheet.name,\n      filesCreated,\n      files: createdFiles,\r\n    });\r\n  } catch (err) {\r\n    console.error(\"[Create Folder] Fatal error:\", err.message);\r\n    return res\r\n      .status(500)\r\n      .json({ error: err.message || \"Internal server error\" });\r\n  }\r\n}\r\n\r\nmodule.exports = {\r\n  importPlaylist,\r\n  getSheet,\r\n  getAllSheets,\r\n  deleteSheet,\r\n  renameSheet,\r\n  createFolderFromSheet,\r\n};\r\n"
          },

            "leetcodeService.js": "const axios = require(\"axios\");\r\n\r\n/**\r\n * leetcodeService — fetches full problem data from LeetCode's public GraphQL API.\r\n */\r\n\r\nconst   .trim();\r\n}\r\n\r\nfunction splitTokens(text) {\r\n  const normalized = normalizeText(text);\r\n  if (!normalized) return [];\r\n\r\n  return normalized\r\n    .split(/[\\s-]+/)\r\n    .map((token) => token.trim())\r\n    .filter((token) => token.length >= 2)\r\n    .filter((token) => !/^\\d+$/.test(token))\r\n    .filter((token) => !STOP_WORDS.has(token));\r\n}\r\n\r\nfunction extractFrontendIdHints(text) {\r\n  const hints = new Set();\r\n  const normalized = String(text || \"\");\r\n\r\n  const matchers = [\r\n    /(?:leetcode|lc)\\s*#?\\s*(\\d{1,4})\\b/gi,\r\n    /\\b(?:problem|ques(?:tion)?)\\s*#?\\s*(\\d{1,4})\\b/gi,\r\n    /\\b#(\\d{1,4})\\b/g,\r\n    /\\b(\\d{1,4})\\s*[.\\-:|]\\s*[a-z]/gi,\r\n    /^(\\d{1,4})\\b/gi,\r\n  ];\r\n\r\n  for (const matcher of matchers) {\r\n    for (const match of normalized.matchAll(matcher)) {\r\n      const id = Number(match?.[1]);\r\n      if (!id || id < 1 || id > 4000) continue;\r\n      hints.add(String(id));\r\n    }\r\n  }\r\n\r\n  return hints;\r\n}\r\n\r\n/**\r\n * Fetches full problem data from LeetCode by title slug.\r\n * Returns a simplified problem object or null on failure.\r\n */\r\nasync function question.codeSnippets?.find(\r\n      (s) => s.langSlug === \"javascript\",\r\n    );\r\n    const starterCode =\r\n      jsSnippet?.code || question.codeSnippets?.[0]?.code || \"\";\r\n\r\n    return tokenToProblemIdsCache) {\r\n    return {\r\n      catalog: problemCatalogCache,\r\n      tokenToProblemIds: tokenToProblemIdsCache,\r\n    };\r\n  }\r\n\r\n  const response = await axios.get(LEETCODE_ALL_PROBLEMS_URL, {\r\n    timeout: 20000,\r\n    headers: {\r\n      \"User-Agent\": \"Mozilla/5.0 (compatible; AlgoNoteAI/1.0)\",\r\n    },\r\n  });\r\n\r\n  const pairs = response.data?.stat_status_pairs || [];\r\n  const catalog = [];\r\n  const tokenToProblemIds = new Map();\r\n\r\n  for (const item of pairs) {\r\n    const title = String(item?.stat?.question__title || \"\").trim();\r\n    const titleSlug = item?.stat?.question__title_slug;\r\n    const frontendId = String(item?.stat?.frontend_question_id || \"\").trim();\r\n    const difficultyLevel = Number(item?.difficulty?.level || 0);\r\n\r\n    if (!title || !titleSlug || !frontendId) continue;\r\n\r\n    const tokens = splitTokens(title);\r\n    const problem = {\r\n      title,\r\n      titleSlug,\r\n      frontendId,\r\n      difficulty:\r\n        difficultyLevel === 1\r\n          ? \"Easy\"\r\n          : difficultyLevel === 2\r\n            ? \"Medium\"\r\n            : (idHints.size > 0) {\r\n    if (idHints.has(problem.frontendId)) {\r\n      score += 0.8;\r\n    } else {\r\n      score -= 0.25;\r\n    }\r\n  }\r\n\r\n  if (problem.normalizedTitle === queryNormalized) {\r\n    score += 1;\r\n  } else if (queryNormalized.includes(problem.normalizedTitle)) {\r\n    score += 0.35;\r\n  } else if (problem.normalizedTitle.includes(queryNormalized)) {\r\n    score += 0.2;\r\n  }\r\n\r\n  let overlap = 0;\r\n  for (const token of queryTokens) {\r\n    if (problem.tokenSet.has(token)) overlap += 1;\r\n  }\r\n\r\n  const recall = overlap / queryTokens.length;\r\n  const precision = overlap / Math.max(problem.tokenSet.size, 1);\r\n  score += recall * 0.55 + precision * 0.35;\r\n\r\n  if (overlap >= 2) score += 0.1;\r\n  if (overlap === queryTokens.length && overlap > 0) score += 0.2;\r\n\r\n  return Math.max(0, Math.min(score, 1));\r\n}\r\n\r\nasync function findProblemCandidatesByTitle(videoTitle, limit = 5) {\r\n  const }\r\n    }\r\n\r\n    const scored = [];\r\n\r\n    for (const id of candidateProblemIds) {\r\n      const problem = catalog[id];\r\n      const score = scoreTitleMatch(\r\n        queryNormalized,\r\n        queryTokens,\r\n        idHints,\r\n        problem,\r\n      );\r\n      if (score < 0.35) continue;\r\n\r\n      scored.push({\r\n        title: problem.title,\r\n        titleSlug: problem.titleSlug,\r\n        frontendId: problem.frontendId,\r\n        difficulty: problem.difficulty,\r\n        score: Number(score.toFixed(3)),\r\n      });\r\n    }\r\n\r\n    scored.sort((a, b) => b.score - a.score);\r\n    return scored.slice(0, Math.max(1, limit));\r\n  } catch (err) {\r\n    console.error(\r\n      `LeetCode candidate match error for title \")\r\n    .trim();\r\n}\r\n\r\nfunction formatCandidateContext(candidateProblems = []) {\r\n  if (!Array.isArray(candidateProblems) || candidateProblems.length === 0) {\r\n    return \"None\";\r\n https://www.youtube.com/playlist?list=PLxxxx\r\n *  - https://youtube.com/playlist?list=PLxxxx\r\n */\r\nfunction extractPlaylistId(url) {\r\n  try {\r\n    const parsed = new URL(url);\r\n    const listParam = parsed.searchParams.get(\"list\");\r\n    if (!listParam) throw new Error(\"No playlist ID found in URL\");\r\n    return listParam;\r\n  } catch (err) {\r\n    throw new Error(`Invalid YouTube playlist URL: ${err.message}`);\r\n  }\r\n}\r\n\r\n/**\r\n * Fetches all videos from a playlist, handling pagination automatically.\r\n * Returns an array of { videoTitle, videoUrl } objects.\r\n */\r\nasync function fetchPlaylistVideos(playlistUrl) {\r\n  if (!YOUTUBE_API_KEY) {\r\n    throw new Error(\"YOUTUBE_API_KEY is not set in environment variables\");\r\n  }\r\n\r\n  const playlistId = extractPlaylistId(playlistUrl);\r\n  const videos = [];\r\n  let nextPageToken = null;\r\n\r\n  do {\r\n    const params = {\r\n      part: \"snippet\",\r\n      playlistId,\r\n      maxResults: 50,\r\n      key: YOUTUBE_API_KEY,\r\n    };\r\n    if (nextPageToken) params.pageToken = nextPageToken;\r\n\r\n    const response = await axios.get(`${YOUTUBE_API_BASE}/playlistItems`, {\r\n      params,\r\n    });\r\n    const items = response.data.items || [];\r\n\r\n    for (const item of items) {\r\n      const snippet = item.snippet;\r\n      const videoId = snippet?.resourceId?.videoId;\r\n      if (!videoId) continue;\r\n\r\n      videos.push({\r\n        videoTitle: snippet.title,\r\n        videoUrl: `https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=${videoId}`,\r\n      });\r\n    }\r\n\r\n    nextPageToken = response.data.nextPageToken || null;\r\n  } while (nextPageToken);\r\n\r\n  return videos;\r\n}\r\n\r\nmodule.exports = { fetchPlaylistVideos };\r\n"
          }
        }

MoreHorizontal,\n  Trash2,\n} from \"lucide-react\";\nimport { useLocation, useNavigate } from \"react-router-dom\";\nimport useFileStore from \"../../store/useFileStore\";\nimport { getFileVisualType         "LoginPage.jsx": "import React, { useState } from \"react\";\nimport { useClerk, useSignIn } from \"@clerk/react\";\nimport { Link, useNavigate } from \"react-router-dom\";\nimport heroImage from \"./hero (1).webp\";\nimport \"./LoginPage.css\";\n\nconst isValidEmail = (value) => /^[^\\s@]+@[^\\s@]+\\.[^\\s@]+$/.test(value.trim());\n\nconst resolveVerificationRedirect = (verification) => {\n  const url = verification?.externalVerificationRedirectURL;\n  return url ? url.toString() : \"\";\n};\n\r\nconst LoginPage = () => {\r\n  const navigate = useNavigate();\r\n  const clerk = useClerk();\r\n  const { signIn } = useSignIn();\r\n  const appOrigin = window.location.origin;\r\n  const [formData, setFormData] = useState({\r\n    email: \"\",\r\n    password: \"\",\r\n  });\r\n  const [isFormSubmitting, setIsFormSubmitting] = useState(false);\r\n  const [isGoogleLoading, setIsGoogleLoading] = useState(false);\r\n  const [errorMessage, setErrorMessage] = useState(\"\");\r\n\r\n  const handleChange = (e) => {\r\n    const { name, value } = e.target;\r\n    setFormData((prev) => ({\r\n      ...prev,\r\n      [name]: value,\r\n    }));\r\n  };\r\n\r\n  const handleSubmit = (e) => {\r\n    e.preventDefault();\r\n\r\n    if (!clerk?.loaded || !signIn || isFormSubmitting || isGoogleLoading) {\r\n      return;\r\n    }\r\n\r\n    const signInWithPassword = async () => {\n      const normalizedEmail = formData.email.trim();\n\n      if (!isValidEmail(normalizedEmail)) {\n        setErrorMessage(\"Please enter a valid email address.\");\n        return;\n      }\n\n      setIsFormSubmitting(true);\n      setErrorMessage(\"\");\n\n      try {\n        const result = await signIn.create({\n          identifier: normalizedEmail,\n          password: formData.password,\n        });\n\r\n        if (result.status === \"complete\") {\r\n          await clerk.setActive({ session: result.createdSessionId });\r\n          navigate(\"/\", { replace: true });\r\n          return;\r\n        }\r\n\r\n        setErrorMessage(\"Additional verification is required to continue.\");\r\n      } catch (error) {\r\n        const fallbackMessage =\r\n          \"Unable to sign in. Please check your credentials.\";\r\n        setErrorMessage(error?.errors?.[0]?.longMessage || fallbackMessage);\r\n      } finally {\r\n        setIsFormSubmitting(false);\r\n      }\r\n    };\r\n\r\n    signInWithPassword();\r\n  };\r\n\r\n  const handleGoogleSignIn = async () => {\n    if (isGoogleLoading || isFormSubmitting) {\r\n      return;\r\n    }\r\n\r\n    setIsGoogleLoading(true);\r\n    setErrorMessage(\"\");\r\n\r\n    try {\r\n      const signInResource = clerk?.client?.signIn ?? signIn;\r\n\r\n      if (!signInResource) {\r\n        throw new Error(\r\n          \"Authentication is not initialized yet.         "SignUpPageCustom.jsx": "import React, { useState } from \"react\";\r\nimport { useClerk, useSignUp } from \"@clerk/react\";\r\nimport { Link, useNavigate } from \"react-router-dom\";\r\nimport heroImage from \"./hero (1).webp\";\nimport \"./LoginPage.css\";\n\nconst isValidEmail = (value) => /^[^\\s@]+@[^\\s@]+\\.[^\\s@]+$/.test(value.trim());\n\nconst resolveVerificationRedirect = (verification) => {\n  const url = verification?.externalVerificationRedirectURL;\n  return url ? Please refresh and try again.\");\r\n      }\r\n\r\n      const redirectUrl = `${appOrigin}/sign-in/sso-callback`;\r\n      const actionCompleteRedirectUrl = `${appOrigin}/`;\r\n\r\n      if (typeof signUpResource.authenticateWithRedirect === \"function\") {\r\n        await signUpResource.authenticateWithRedirect({\r\n          strategy: \"oauth_google\",\r\n          redirectUrl,\r\n          actionCompleteRedirectUrl,\r\n        });\r\n        return;\r\n      }\r\n\r\n      const result = await signUpResource.create({\r\n        strategy: \"oauth_google\",\r\n        redirectUrl,\r\n        actionCompleteRedirectUrl,\r\n      });\r\n      const nextUrl = resolveVerificationRedirect(\r\n        result.verifications?.externalAccount,\r\n      );\r\n\r\n      if (!nextUrl) {\r\n        throw new Error(\"Google sign up could not be started.\");\r\n      }\r\n\r\n      window.location.assign(nextUrl);\r\n      return;\r\n    } catch (error) {\r\n      const fallbackMessage = \"Google sign up failed. 0.2),\r\n    },\r\n    { name: \"Binary Search\", solved: Math.round(medium * 0.1 + easy * 0.1) },\r\n    { name: \"Graph\", solved: Math.round(medium * 0.1 + hard * 0.2) },\r\n    { name: \"Trie\", solved: Math.round(hard * 0.1) },\r\n    { name: \"Backtracking\", solved: Math.round(medium * 0.05 + hard * 0.1) },\r\n  ];\r\n};\r\n\r\nconst calculateVerdict = ({ easySolved, mediumSolved, hardSolved }) => {\n  const rawScore = easySolved * 1 + mediumSolved * 2 + hardSolved * 3;\r\n  const MAX_RAW_SCORE = 1500;\r\n  const score = Math.min((rawScore / MAX_RAW_SCORE) * 100, 100);\r\n\r\n  let level = \"Beginner Level\";\r\n  let message =\r\n    \"Focus on building foundational knowledge. Solve more easy problems to grasp core concepts.\";\r\n  if (score >= 70) {\r\n    level = \"SDE Interview Ready\";\r\n    message =\r\n      \"You have a strong grasp of DSA! Focus on hard problems and mock interviews to sharpen your edge.\";\r\n  } else if (score >= 40) {\r\n    level = \"Intermediate Level\";\r\n    message =\r\n      \"Good progress! Start focusing on medium problems and topics like DP and Graphs to level up.\";\r\n  }\r\n  return { score, level, message };\n};\n\nconst PROFILE_ANALYSIS_STORAGE_PREFIX = \"profile-analysis:last:\";\n\r\n// ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────\r\nconst ProfileAnalysisPage = () => {\n  const { isSignedIn, userId } = useAuth();\n  const [profileData, setProfileData] = useState(null);\n  const [topics, setTopics] = useState(null);\r\n  const [isLoading, setIsLoading] = useState(false);\r\n  const [error, setError] = useState(null);\r\n  const [verdict, setVerdict] = useState(null);\r\n  const [recommendations, setRecommendations] = useState(null);\r\n  const [currentUsername, setCurrentUsername] = useState(\"\");\r\n  const [revisionSheetRows, setRevisionSheetRows] = useState([]);\r\n  const [isImporting, setIsImporting] = useState(false);\n  const [importResult, setImportResult] = useState(null);\n  const storageKey = useMemo(\n    () => (userId ? `${PROFILE_ANALYSIS_STORAGE_PREFIX}${userId}` : null),\n    [userId],\n  );\n\n  useEffect(() => {\n    if (!isSignedIn || !storageKey) {\n      return;\n    }\n\n    try {\n      const raw = window.localStorage.getItem(storageKey);\n      if (!raw) return;\n      const saved = JSON.parse(raw);\n\n      setProfileData(saved.profileData || null);\n      setTopics(saved.topics || null);\n      setVerdict(saved.verdict || null);\n      setRecommendations(saved.recommendations || null);\n      setCurrentUsername(saved.currentUsername || \"\");\n      setRevisionSheetRows(saved.revisionSheetRows || []);\n      setImportResult(saved.importResult || null);\n      setError(null);\n    } catch (_error) {\n      window.localStorage.removeItem(storageKey);\n    }\n  }, [isSignedIn, storageKey]);\n\n  useEffect(() => {\n    if (!isSignedIn || !storageKey || !profileData || !currentUsername) {\n      return;\n    }\n\n    const payload = {\n      profileData,\n      topics,\n      verdict,\n      recommendations,\n      currentUsername,\n      revisionSheetRows,\n      importResult,\n    };\n\n    window.localStorage.setItem(storageKey, JSON.stringify(payload));\n  }, [\n    currentUsername,\n    importResult,\n    isSignedIn,\n    profileData,\n    recommendations,\n    revisionSheetRows,\n    storageKey,\n    topics,\n    verdict,\n  ]);\n\n  const handleAnalyze = async (username) => {\n    if (!username.trim()) return;\r\n    setIsLoading(true);\r\n    setError(null);\r\n    setProfileData(null);\r\n    setRevisionSheetRows([]);\r\n\r\n    try {\r\n      const { data } = await profileAnalysisApi.analyzeProfile(username.trim());\r\n\r\n      const normalised = {\r\n        totalSolved: data.totalSolved ?? 0,\r\n        easySolved: data.easySolved ?? 0,\r\n        mediumSolved: data.mediumSolved ?? 0,\r\n        hardSolved: data.hardSolved ?? 0,\r\n        acceptanceRate:\r\n          data.acceptanceRate != null\r\n            ? parseFloat(data.acceptanceRate).toFixed(1)\r\n            : \"N/A\",\r\n        ranking: data.ranking ?? 0,\r\n        contestRating: data.contributionPoints ?? data.reputation ?? 0,\r\n      };\r\n\r\n      const derivedTopics = buildTopics(\r\n        normalised.easySolved,\r\n        normalised.mediumSolved,\r\n        normalised.hardSolved,\r\n      );\r\n      const verdictData = calculateVerdict(normalised);\r\n\r\n      const weakTopicNames = derivedTopics\r\n        .filter((t) => t.solved <= 20)\r\n        .map((t) => t.name);\r\n      let filteredRecs = {};\r\n      try {\r\n        const recRes = await profileAnalysisApi.getRecommendations({\r\n          weakAreas: weakTopicNames,\r\n          limit: 20,\r\n        });\r\n        filteredRecs = recRes.data?.data || {};\r\n      } catch (e) {\r\n        filteredRecs = {};\r\n      }\r\n\r\n      setProfileData(normalised);\r\n      setTopics(derivedTopics);\r\n      setVerdict(verdictData);\r\n      setRecommendations(filteredRecs);\n      setCurrentUsername(username.trim().toLowerCase());\n      setImportResult(null);\n    } catch (err) {\n      const msg =\r\n        err.response?.data?.error ||\r\n        err.message ||\r\n        \"Failed to fetch profile. Check username and try again.\";\r\n      setError(msg);\r\n    } finally {\r\n      setIsLoading(false);\r\n    }\n  };\n\r\n  // Saves a single problem to the revision list (MongoDB via problem.problemName || problem.name;\r\n    const leetcodeUrl = problem.leetcodeUrl || problem.url || \"\";\r\n    const topicFolderName = topic || \"Recommended\";\r\n\r\n    await Object.entries(recommendations).forEach(([topic, probs]) => {\r\n        probs.forEach((p) => {\r\n          problems.push({\r\n            topic,\r\n            problemName: p.name,\r\n            difficulty: p.difficulty || \"Medium\",\r\n            leetcodeUrl: p.leetcodeUrl || p.url || \"\",\r\n          });\r\n        });\r\n      });\r\n      const res = await           "RecommendationSection.jsx": "import React, { useState } from \"react\";\nimport {\n  ChevronDown,\n  ChevronUp,\n  Download,\n  ExternalLink,\n  FolderPlus,\n  Loader2,\n  Sparkles,\n} from \"lucide-react\";\nimport profileAnalysisApi from \"../../services/profileAnalysisApi\";\n\nconst getDifficultyColor = (difficulty) => {\n  switch ((difficulty || \"\").toLowerCase()) {\n    case \"easy\":\n      return \"border-emerald-400/15 bg-emerald-500/10 text-emerald-300\";\n    case \"medium\":\n      return \"border-amber-400/15 bg-amber-500/10 text-amber-300\";\n    case \"hard\":\n      return \"border-rose-400/15 bg-rose-500/10 text-rose-300\";\n    default:\n      return \"border-white/10 bg-white/[0.04] text-white/65\";\n  }\n};\n\nconst TopicQuestionRow = ({ index, problem, onAdd, addState }) => {\n  const practiceUrl = problem.leetcodeUrl || problem.url;\n\n  return (\n    <div className=\"flex items-center gap-3 border-b border-white/8 px-3 py-2.5 transition-colors last:border-b-0 hover:bg-white/[0.025]\">\n      <div className=\"flex h-7 w-7 shrink-0 items-center justify-center rounded-full border border-white/10 bg-white/[0.04] text-[11px] font-semibold text-white/60\">\n        {index + 1}\n      </div>\n\n      <span className=\"min-w-0 flex-1 truncate text-sm font-medium text-white/92\">\n        {problem.problemName || problem.name}\n      </span>\n\n      <div className=\"flex w-24 shrink-0 justify-center\">\n        <span\n          className={`rounded-full border px-2.5 py-1 text-xs font-semibold ${getDifficultyColor(\n            problem.difficulty,\n          )}`}\n        >\n          {problem.difficulty || \"Unknown\"}\n        </span>\n      </div>\n\n      {practiceUrl ?         "api.js": "import axios from \"axios\";\n\nlet authTokenGetter = null;\nlet authUserIdGetter = null;\n\nconst isBrowser = typeof window !== \"undefined\";\nconst devApiBaseUrl =\n  isBrowser && import.meta.env.DEV\n    ? `${window.location.protocol}//${window.location.hostname}:5001/api`\n    : \"/api\";\n\nexport const setAuthTokenGetter = (getter) => {\n  authTokenGetter = getter;\n};\n\r\nexport const setAuthUserIdGetter = (getter) => {\r\n  authUserIdGetter = getter;\r\n};\r\n\nconst api = axios.create({\n  baseURL: devApiBaseUrl,\n  headers: {\n    \"Content-Type\": \"application/json\",\n  },\n});\n\nconst RETRY_DELAYS_MS = [500, 1200, 2500, 4000, 6000, 8000];\n\nconst shouldRetryRequest = (error) => {\n  const status = error?.response?.status;\n  const code = error?.code;\n\n  return status === 502 || code === \"ERR_NETWORK\" || code === \"ECONNABORTED\";\n};\n\nconst wait = (delay) =>\n  new Promise((resolve) => {\n    window.setTimeout(resolve, delay);\n  });\n\nconst withRetry = async (requestFn) => {\n  let lastError = null;\n\n  for (let attempt = 0; attempt <= RETRY_DELAYS_MS.length; attempt += 1) {\n    try {\n      return await requestFn();\n    } catch (error) {\n      lastError = error;\n      if (\n        attempt === RETRY_DELAYS_MS.length ||\n        !shouldRetryRequest(error)\n      ) {\n        break;\n      }\n\n      await wait(RETRY_DELAYS_MS[attempt]);\n    }\n  }\n\n  throw lastError;\n};\n\r\napi.interceptors.request.use(async (config) => {\r\n  if (authTokenGetter) {\r\n    const token = await authTokenGetter();\r\n    if (token) {\r\n      config.headers.Authorization = `Bearer ${token}`;\r\n    }\r\n  }\r\n\r\n  if (authUserIdGetter) {\r\n    const userId = await authUserIdGetter();\r\n    if (userId) {\r\n      config.headers[\"x-user-id\"] = userId;\r\n    }\r\n  }\r\n\r\n  return config;\r\n});\r\n\r\nexport const fileService = {\n  getFileSystem: () => api.get(\"/files\"),\n  createFileNode: (name, type, parentId, link) =>\r\n    api.post(\"/files\", { name, type, parentId, link }),\r\n  deleteFileNode: (id) => api.delete(`/files/${id}`),\r\n  updateFileNode: (id, data) => api.put(`/files/${id}`, data),\r\n  getProblem: (fileId) => api.get(`/problems/${fileId}`),\r\n  createProblem: (fileId) => api.post(\"/problems\", { fileId }),\r\n  updateProblem: (fileId, data) => api.put(`/problems/${fileId}`, data),\r\n  analyzeCode: (code, language) => api.post(\"/ai/analyze\", { code, language }),\n  importProblem: (url) => api.post(\"/problems/import\", { url }),\n};\n\nexport const statsService = {\n  getLoginStats: () => withRetry(() => api.get(\"/stats/logins\")),\n  recordLogin: (sessionId) =>\n    withRetry(() => api.post(\"/stats/logins\", { sessionId })),\n};\n\nexport default api;\n",

        "useFileStore.js": "import { create } from \"zustand\";\nimport { fileService } from \"../services/api\";\nimport {\n  findTreeNode,\n  removeTreeNode,\n  updateTreeNode,\n} from \"../utils/fileTree\";\n\nconst FILE_SYSTEM_RETRY_DELAYS_MS = [500, 1200, 2500, 4000, 6000, 8000, 10000];\nlet loadFileSystemPromise = null;\n\nconst defaultSolutionEntries = () => [\n  {\n    id: \"optimal\",\n    label: \"Optimal\",\n    code: \"\",\n  },\n];\n\nconst normalizeSolutionEntries = (item = {}) => {\n  if (Array.isArray(item.solutionEntries) && item.solutionEntries.length > 0) {\n    return item.solutionEntries;\n  }\n\n  const legacyEntries = [\n    { id: \"brute\", label: \"Brute Force\", code: item.solutions?.brute || \"\" },\n    { id: \"better\", label: \"Better\", code: item.solutions?.better || \"\" },\n    { id: \"optimal\", label: \"Optimal\", code: item.solutions?.optimal || \"\" },\n  ].filter((entry) => entry.code);\n\n  return legacyEntries.length > 0 ? response.data : [],\n            isLoading: false,\n            error: null,\n            hasLoadedFileSystem: true,\n          });\n          return true;\n        } catch (error) {\n          lastError = error;\n          if (\n            attempt === FILE_SYSTEM_RETRY_DELAYS_MS.length ||\n            !shouldRetryFileSystemLoad(error)\n          ) {\n            break;\n          }\n\n          await wait(FILE_SYSTEM_RETRY_DELAYS_MS[attempt]);\n        }\n      }\n\n      const message =\n        lastError?.response?.data?.message ||\n        lastError?.message ||\n        \"Failed to load file system.\";\n\n      set({\n        fileSystem: [],\n        activeFileId: null,\n        error: message,\n        isLoading: false,\n        hasLoadedFileSystem: false,\n      });\n      console.error(\"Failed to load file system\", lastError);\n      return false;\n    })();\n\n    try {\n      return await loadFileSystemPromise;\n    } finally {\n      loadFileSystemPromise = null;\n    }\n  },\n\n  setActiveFile: async (fileId) => {\n    set({ activeFileId: fileId });\n    // When selecting a file, ensure we have its latest content/problem details\n    // We could eager load or lazy load. For now, we find it in tree, if content is missing, we might need to fetch.\n    // However, our getFileSystem might be shallow? Use getProblem for details.\n\n    // Find file type\n    const file = findTreeNode(get().fileSystem, fileId);\n    if (file && file.type === \"file\") {\n      // Always fetch full problem details to ensure we have latest data\n      try {\n        const res = await fileService.getProblem(fileId);\n        // Merge problem details into store\n        set((state) => ({\n          fileSystem: updateTreeNode(state.fileSystem, fileId, (item) => ({\n            ...item,\n            ...res.data,\n            id: item.id,\n            name: item.name,\n            type: item.type,\n            parentId: item.parentId,\n          })),\n        }));\n        console.log(\"✅ Problem data refreshed for file:\", fileId);\n      } catch (err) {\n        console.error(\"Failed to load problem details\", err);\n      }\n    }\n  },\n\n  toggleFolder: (folderId) =>\n    set((state) => {\n      const isExpanded = state.expandedFolders.includes(folderId);\n      return {\n        expandedFolders: isExpanded\n          ? state.expandedFolders.filter((id) => id !== folderId)\n          : [...state.expandedFolders, folderId],\n      };\n    }),\n\n  // Clear expanded folders to reduce clutter\n  clearExpandedFolders: () => set({ expandedFolders: [] }),\n\n  // Add Item (API Call)\n  addItem: async (parentId, name, type, link) => {\n    try {\n      set({ error: null });\n      const res = await fileService.createFileNode(name, type, parentId, link);\n      const newItem = res.data;\n      // Removed: Backend uses 'id' (Postgres), not '_id' (Mongo)\n\n      set((state) => {\n        const addItemRecursive = (items) => {\n          // If adding to root (parentId null)\n          if (!parentId) return [...items, newItem];\n\n          return items.map((item) => {\n            if (item.id === parentId) {\n              return { ...item, children: [...(item.children || []), newItem] };\n            }\n            if (item.children) {\n              return { ...item, children: addItemRecursive(item.children) };\n            }\n            return item;\n          });\n        };\n\n        // Special handling if parentId is null (add to root)\n        if (!parentId) {\n          return { fileSystem: [...state.fileSystem, newItem] };\n        }\n\n        return { fileSystem: addItemRecursive(state.fileSystem) };\n      });\n      return newItem; // Return the created item for usage\n    } catch (error) {\n      const message = error.response?.data?.message || error.message;\n      set({ error: message });\n      console.error(\"Failed to add item\", error);\n      return null;\n    }\n  },\n\n  deleteItem: async (itemId) => {\n    try {\n      await fileService.deleteFileNode(itemId);\n      set((state) => ({\n        fileSystem: removeTreeNode(state.fileSystem, itemId),\n      }));\n    } catch (error) {\n      console.error(\"Failed to delete item\", error);\n    }\n  },\n\n  // Update Content (solutions)\n  updateFileContent: async (fileId, solutionType, newContent) => {\n    // Optimistic update\n    set((state) => {\n      return {\n        fileSystem: updateTreeNode(state.fileSystem, fileId, (item) => ({\n          ...item,\n          solutionEntries: normalizeSolutionEntries(item).map((entry) =>\n            entry.id === solutionType ? { ...entry, code: newContent } : entry,\n          ),\n call\n    try {\n      await fileService.updateProblem(fileId, {\n        solutionEntries: normalizeSolutionEntries(\n          findTreeNode(get().fileSystem, fileId),\n        ).map((entry) =>\n          entry.id === solutionType ? { ...entry, code: newContent } : entry,\n        ),\n      });\n    } catch (error) {\n      console.error(\"Failed to save content\", error);\n    }\n  },\n\n  updateFileNotes: async (fileId, notes) => {\n    // Optimistic\n    set((state) => {\n      return {\n        fileSystem: updateTreeNode(state.fileSystem, fileId, (item) => ({\n          ...item,\n          notes,\n        })),\n      };\n    });\n\n    await fileService.updateProblem(fileId, { notes });\n  },\n\n  updateFileLink: async (fileId, link) => {\n    // Optimistic\n    set((state) => {\n      return {\n        fileSystem: updateTreeNode(state.fileSystem, fileId, (item) => ({\n          ...item,\n          link,\n        })),\n      };\n    });\n\n    await mergeProblemDetails: (fileId, details) =>\n    set((state) => ({\n      fileSystem: updateTreeNode(state.fileSystem, fileId, (item) => ({\n        ...item,\n        ...details,\n        solutionEntries:\n          details.solutionEntries ??\n          item.solutionEntries ??\n          defaultSolutionEntries(),\n        analysis: {\n          time: details.analysis?.time ?? ?? \"\",\n        },\n        solutions: {\n          brute: details.solutions?.brute ?? item.solutions?.brute ?? \"\",\n          better: details.solutions?.better ?? item.solutions?.better ?? \"\",\n          optimal: details.solutions?.optimal ?? item.solutions?.optimal ?? \"\",\n        },\n      })),\n    })),\n\n  updateFileFlags: async (fileId, flags) => {\n    set((state) => ({\n      fileSystem: updateTreeNode(state.fileSystem, fileId, (item) => ({\n        ...item,\n        ...flags,\n      })),\n    }));\n\n    await fileService.updateFileNode(fileId, flags);\n  },\n\n  toggleFileRevision: async (fileId) => {\n    const current = findTreeNode(get().fileSystem, fileId);\n    if (!current) {\n      return;\n    }\n\n    await get().updateFileFlags(fileId, { isRevised: !current.isRevised });\n  },\n\n  toggleFileSolved: async (fileId) => {\n    const current = findTreeNode(get().fileSystem, fileId);\n    if (!current) {\n      return;\n    }\n\n    await     return;\n    }\n\n    await get().updateFileFlags(fileId, { isImportant: !current.isImportant });\n  },\n\n  updateSolutionEntries: async (fileId, solutionEntries) => {\n    set((state) => ({\n         "fileTree.js": "export function findTreeNode(nodes, targetId) {\n  for (const node of nodes) {\n    if (String(node.id) === String(targetId)) {\n      return node;\n    }\n\n    if (node.children?.length) {\n      const found = findTreeNode(node.children, targetId);\n      if (found) {\n        return found;\n      }\n    }\n  }\n\n  return null;\n}\n\nexport function updateTreeNode(nodes, targetId, updater) {\n  return nodes.map((node) => {\n    if (String(node.id) === String(targetId)) {\n      return updater(node);\n    }\n\n    if (node.children?.length) {\n      return {\n        ...node,\n        children: updateTreeNode(node.children, targetId, updater),\n      };\n    }\n\n    return node;\n  });\n}\n\nexport function removeTreeNode(nodes, targetId) {\n  return nodes\n    .filter((node) => String(node.id) !== String(targetId))\n    .map((node) => {\n      if (!node.children?.length) {\n        return node;\n      }\n\n      return {\n        ...node,\n        children: removeTreeNode(node.children, targetId),\n      };\n    });\n}\n",
        "problemSources.js": "const titleCaseFromSlug = (slug = \"\") =>\n  slug\n    .split(\"-\")\n    .filter(Boolean)\n    .map((part) => part.charAt(0).toUpperCase() + part.slice(1))\n    .join(\" \");\n\nexport const detectProblemSource = (link = \"\") => {\n  try {\n    const parsed = new URL(link);\n    const host = parsed.hostname.toLowerCase();\n\n    if (host.endsWith(\"leetcode.com\") && /\\/problems\\//i.test(parsed.pathname)) {\n      return \"leetcode\";\n    }\n\n    if (\n      (host === \"geeksforgeeks.org\" ||\n        host === \"www.geeksforgeeks.org\" ||\n        host === \"practice.geeksforgeeks.org\") &&\n      /\\/problems?\\//i.test(parsed.pathname)\n    ) {\n      return \"gfg\";\n    }\n  } catch (_error) {\n    return null;\n  }\n\n  return null;\n};\n\nexport const extractProblemNameFromLink = (link = \"\") => {\n  const source = detectProblemSource(link);\n  if (!source) {\n    return \"\";\n  }\n\n  try {\n    const parsed = new URL(link);\n    const segments = parsed.pathname.split(\"/\").filter(Boolean);\n\n    if (source === \"leetcode\") {\n      const match = link.match(/leetcode\\.com\\/problems\\/([^/]+)/i);\n      return match?.[1] ? titleCaseFromSlug(match[1]) : \"\";\n    }\n\n    const problemIndex = segments.findIndex((segment) => /^problems?$/i.test(segment));\n    const slug =\n      problemIndex >= 0 && problemIndex + 1 < segments.length\n        ? segments[problemIndex + 1]\n        : segments.filter((segment) => !/^\\d+$/.test(segment)).at(-1) || \"\";\n\n    return titleCaseFromSlug(slug);\n  } catch (_error) {\n    return \"\";\n  }\n};\n\nexport const getProblemSourceLabel = (source) => {\n  if (source === \"leetcode\") {\n    return \"LeetCode\";\n  }\n\n  if (source === \"gfg\") {\n    return \"GFG\";\n  }\n\n  return \"Problem\";\n};\n\nexport const isNotesFileName = (name = \"\") => /\\.txt$/i.test(String(name).trim());\n\nexport const stripNotesExtension = (name = \"\") =>\n  String(name).replace(/\\.txt$/i, \"\").trim();\n\nexport const ensureNotesFileName = (name = \"\") => {\n  const baseName = stripNotesExtension(name);\n  return baseName ?
